Freq: 3: Low

 :       : The player's name and trainer type are chosen 
 :       : automatically.

@>Control Self Switch: A =ON
@>Transfer Player:[008: Nightmare], (014,084), Up, No Fade
@>Script: pbToneChangeAll(Tone.new(0,0,0,0),20)

@>Text: \bProfessor Hideki: Why not have a little pop quiz? There's a prize in it, if you win.
@>Show Choices: Yes, No
(When Cancel: Choice 2)
: When [Yes]
 @>Script: pbSetExpression
 @>Text: Zyro: Bring it on.
 @>Control Variables: [0005: Temp Text Entry] = 0
 @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
 @>Text: \bProfessor Hideki: Alright, first question! Who founded the Dark Rising Head Quarters?
 @>Show Choices: Jean Blake, Dark Rising Girl, Hoopa
 (When Cancel: Disallow)
 : When [Jean Blake]
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bCorrect! Though we don't have the whereabouts of Blake, his deeds have been recorded down in our history books.
  @>
 : When [Dark Rising Girl]
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bYou would think that's the answer, huh? So close, but you'll have to try again.
  @>Control Variables: [0005: Temp Text Entry] += 1
  @>
 : When [Hoopa]
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bWrong, shame on you Zyro.
  @>Control Variables: [0005: Temp Text Entry] += 1
  @>
 : Branch End
 @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
 @>Text: \bNext question! What must you do first before attempting to recruit a Pokemon?
 @>Show Choices: Just catch the damn thing., Weaken them., I forgot.
 (When Cancel: Disallow)
 : When [Just catch the damn thing.]
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bWell, you won't get anything that way.
  @>Control Variables: [0005: Temp Text Entry] += 1
  @>
 : When [Weaken them.]
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bThat's correct! A Pokemon will continue to get stronger if you don't weaken it first.
  @>
 : When [I forgot.]
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bWell, someone needs to pay attention in class.
  @>Control Variables: [0005: Temp Text Entry] += 1
  @>
 : Branch End
 @>Conditional Branch: Variable [0005: Temp Text Entry] == 2
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bThat's too bad. Let me know if you want to try again.
  @>Exit Event Processing
  @>
 : Branch End
 @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
 @>Text: \bLast but not least! What is the fall of humanity called?
 @>Show Choices: Hoopa will get his ass kicked!, The Black Plague, The Nine Year Calamity
 (When Cancel: Disallow)
 : When [Hoopa will get his ass kicked!]
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bHaha, no. I like your motivation, but let's be appropriate.
  @>Control Variables: [0005: Temp Text Entry] += 1
  @>
 : When [The Black Plague]
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bThat was in 1340, a little over six hundred years ago. While the trainers' curse and those of the undead didn't kill as many as the Black Plague, it was still a 
   :    : quarter of that.
  @>Control Variables: [0005: Temp Text Entry] += 1
  @>
 : When [The Nine Year Calamity]
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bCorrect! Nine years ago, all hell broke loose, and people and Pokemon turned on each other.
  @>
 : Branch End
 @>Conditional Branch: Variable [0005: Temp Text Entry] == 2
  @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
  @>Text: \bThat's too bad. Let me know if you want to try again.
  @>Exit Event Processing
  @>
 : Branch End
 @>Control Variables: [0030: Temp Talking Event] = 2
 @>Text: \bWell, you've clearly been studying. Keep up the good work!
 @>Conditional Branch: Self Switch B == OFF
  @>Script: pbReceiveItem(:RARECANDY)
  @>Control Self Switch: B =ON
  @>
 : Branch End
 @>
: When [No]
 @>Script: pbSetExpression
 @>Text: Zyro: Maybe later.
 @>
: Branch End
